                            <p style="margin-top:0in;margin-right:-.1pt;margin-bottom:0in;  margin-left:28.35pt;margin-bottom:.0001pt;text-indent:-28.35pt;line-height:  normal;page-break-after:avoid" class="MsoNormal">
                                <span lang="EN-GB">- Keep this leaflet. You may need to read it
                                    again.</span>
                            </p>
                            <p style="margin-top:0in;margin-right:-.1pt;margin-bottom:0in;  margin-left:28.35pt;margin-bottom:.0001pt;text-indent:-28.35pt;line-height:  normal" class="MsoNormal">
                                <span lang="EN-GB">- If you have any further questions, ask your
                                    doctor or pharmacist.</span>
                            </p>
                            <p style="margin-top:0in;margin-right:-.1pt;margin-bottom:0in;  margin-left:28.35pt;margin-bottom:.0001pt;text-indent:-28.35pt;line-height:  normal" class="MsoNormal">
                                <span lang="EN-GB">- This medicine has been prescribed for you only.
                                    Do not pass it on to others. It may harm them, even if their
                                    signs of illness are the same as yours.</span>
                            </p>
                            <p style="margin-left:28.35pt;text-indent:-28.35pt;line-height:  normal" class="MsoNormal">
                                <span lang="EN-GB">- If you get any side effects, talk to your
                                    doctor or pharmacist. This includes any possible side effects
                                    not listed in this leaflet. See section 4.</span>
                            </p>
                            <p style="margin-right:-.1pt;line-height:normal" class="MsoNormal"/>
                        </div>
          </text>

          <section id="e6514838-d130-476c-8c55-ebadcf47c01c">
            <title value="1.       What Acme Product is and what it is used for"/>
            <code>
              <coding>
                <system value="http://spor.ema.europa.eu/v1/example-sections"/>
                <code value="4"/>
                <display value="1. What X is and what it is used for"/>
              </coding>
            </code>
            <text>
              <status value="additional"/>
              <div xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1999/xhtml">
                                <p style="margin-right:-.1pt;line-height:normal;page-break-after:  avoid" class="MsoNormal"/>
                                <p style="margin-right:-.1pt;line-height:normal;page-break-after:  avoid" class="MsoNormal">
                                    <b>
                                        <span lang="EN-GB">What Acme Product is</span>
                                    </b>
                                </p>
                                <p style="margin-right:-.1pt;line-height:normal;page-break-after:  avoid" class="MsoNormal">
                                    <span lang="EN-GB">Acme Product is a medicine that contains the
                                        active substance dimethyl fumarate. Dimethyl fumarate works
                                        on cells of the immune system (the body's natural defences).
                                        It changes the activity of the immune system and reduces the
                                        production of substances involved in causing
                                        psoriasis.</span>
                                </p>
                                <p style="margin-right:-.1pt;line-height:normal" class="MsoNormal"/>
                                <p style="margin-right:-.1pt;line-height:normal;page-break-after:  avoid" class="MsoNormal">
                                    <b>
                                        <span lang="EN-GB">What Acme Product is used for</span>
                                    </b>
                                </p>
                                <p style="line-height:normal;page-break-after:avoid" class="MsoNormal">
                                    <span lang="EN-GB">Acme Product tablets are used to treat
                                        moderate to severe plaque psoriasis in adults. Psoriasis is
                                        a disease causing thickened, inflamed, red areas on the
                                        skin, often covered by silvery scales.</span>
                                </p>
                                <p style="margin-right:-.1pt;line-height:normal" class="MsoNormal"/>
                                <p style="line-height:normal" class="MsoNormal">
                                    <span lang="EN-GB">Response to Acme Product can be generally
                                        seen as early as week 3 and improves over time. Experience
                                        with related products containing dimethyl fumarate shows
                                        treatment benefit for at least up to 24 months.</span>
                                </p>
                                <p style="margin-right:-.1pt;line-height:normal" class="MsoNormal"/>
                                <p style="margin-right:-.1pt;line-height:normal" class="MsoNormal"/>
                            </div>
            </text>
          </section>
          <section id="8cdfd196-af2c-40a9-bd29-8cbbaf071008">

                            </div>
            </text>
            <section id="df27f760-d5c2-4c25-b6e5-3c89890ff446">
              <title value="Do not take Acme Product"/>
              <code>
                <coding>
                  <system value="http://spor.ema.europa.eu/v1/example-sections"/>
                  <code value="6"/>
                  <display value="Do not &lt;take&gt; &lt;use&gt; X"/>
                </coding>
              </code>
              <text>
                <status value="additional"/>
                <div xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1999/xhtml">
                                    <p style="margin-left:28.35pt;text-indent:-28.35pt;line-height:  normal;page-break-after:avoid" class="MsoNormal">
                                        <span lang="EN-GB">- if you are allergic to dimethyl
                                            fumarate or any of the other ingredients of this
                                            medicine (listed in section 6)</span>
                                    </p>
                                    <p style="margin-left:28.35pt;text-indent:-28.35pt;line-height:  normal" class="MsoNormal">
                                        <span lang="EN-GB">- if you have severe problems with your
                                            stomach or intestines</span>
                                    </p>
                                    <p style="margin-top:0in;margin-right:0in;  margin-bottom:0in;margin-left:28.35pt;text-indent:-28.35pt" class="PrrafodelistaCxSpFirst">
                                        <span style="font-size:11.0pt" lang="EN-GB">-</span>
                                        <span style="font-size:11.0pt" lang="EN-GB">if you have
                                            severe liver or kidney problems</span>
                                    </p>
                                    <p style="margin-top:0in;margin-right:0in;margin-bottom:  0in;margin-left:28.35pt;text-indent:-28.35pt" class="Prrafodelista">
                                        <span style="font-size:11.0pt" lang="EN-GB">-</span>
                                        <span style="font-size:11.0pt" lang="EN-GB">if you are
                                            pregnant or breast-feeding</span>
                                    </p>
                                    <p style="line-height:normal" class="MsoNormal"/>
                                </div>
              </text>
            </section>
            <section id="dd2e0145-a8f2-41a0-b009-1a42fbcf0a6f">
              <title value="Warnings and precautions"/>
              <code>
                <coding>
                  <system value="http://spor.ema.europa.eu/v1/example-sections"/>
                  <code value="7"/>
                  <display value="Warnings and precautions"/>
                </coding>
              </code>
              <text>
                <status value="additional"/>
                <div xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1999/xhtml">
                                    <p style="margin-right:-.1pt;line-height:normal;page-break-after:  avoid" class="MsoNormal">
                                        <span lang="EN-GB">Talk to your doctor or pharmacist before
                                            taking Acme Product.</span>
                                    </p>
                                    <p style="margin-right:-.1pt;line-height:normal" class="MsoNormal"/>
                                    <p style="margin-right:-.1pt;line-height:normal;page-break-after:  avoid" class="MsoNormal">
                                        <u>
                                            <span lang="EN-GB">Monitoring</span>
                                        </u>
                                    </p>
                                    <p style="margin-right:-.1pt;line-height:normal;page-break-after:  avoid" class="MsoNormal">
                                        <span lang="EN-GB">Acme Product</span>
                                        <span lang="EN-GB">may </span>
                                        <span lang="EN-GB">cause problems with your blood, liver or
                                            kidneys. You will have blood and urine tests before
                                            treatment and then regularly during your treatment to
                                            make sure that you are not getting these complications
                                            and can continue to take this medicine</span>
                                        <span lang="EN-GB">. Depending on the results of these blood
                                            and urine tests, your doctor may reduce your dose of
                                            Acme Product or stop treatment.</span>
                                    </p>
                                    <p style="margin-right:-.1pt;line-height:normal" class="MsoNormal"/>
                                    <p style="margin-right:-.1pt;line-height:normal;page-break-after:  avoid" class="MsoNormal">
                                        <u>
                                            <span lang="EN-GB">Infections</span>
                                        </u>
                                    </p>
                                    <p style="line-height:normal;page-break-after:avoid" class="MsoNormal">
                                        <span lang="EN-GB">White blood cells help your body to fight
                                            infections. Acme Product may reduce the number of your
                                            white blood cells. Talk to your doctor if you think you
                                            may have an infection. Symptoms include </span>
                                        <span style="color:#262626" lang="EN-GB">fever, pain, aching
                                            muscles, headache, loss of appetite and a general
                                            feeling of weakness. If you have a serious infection,
                                            either before starting treatment with Acme Product or
                                            during treatment, your doctor may advise you not to take
                                            Acme Product until the infection has resolved.</span>
                                    </p>
                                    <p style="line-height:normal;text-autospace:none" class="MsoNormal">
                                        <u>
                                            <span lang="EN-GB"/>
                                        </u>
                                    </p>
                                    <p style="line-height:normal;page-break-after:avoid" class="MsoNormal">
                                        <u>
                                            <span lang="EN-GB">Gastrointestinal disorders</span>
                                        </u>
                                    </p>
                                    <p style="line-height:normal;page-break-after:avoid" class="MsoNormal">
                                        <span lang="EN-GB">Tell your doctor if you have or have had
                                            problems with your stomach or intestines. Your doctor
                                            will advise you on what care you need to take during
                                            Acme Product treatment.</span>
                                    </p>
                                    <p style="line-height:normal" class="MsoNormal"/>
                                </div>
              </text>
            </section>
            <section id="63c52c6c-e5f5-4126-a63f-37d3e7aa7dea">
              <title value="Children and adolescents"/>
              <code>
                <coding>
                  <system value="http://spor.ema.europa.eu/v1/example-sections"/>
                  <code value="8"/>
                  <display value="Children &lt;and adolescents&gt;"/>
                </coding>
              </code>
              <text>
                <status value="additional"/>
                <div xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1999/xhtml">
                                    <p style="line-height:normal;page-break-after:avoid" class="MsoNormal">
                                        <span lang="EN-GB">Children and adolescents below the age of
                                            18 years should not take this medicine because it has
                                            not been studied in this age group.</span>
                                    </p>
                                    <p style="line-height:normal" class="MsoNormal"/>
                                </div>
              </text>
            </section>
            <section id="2c84d39f-5183-4888-b342-46b036a46558">
              <title value="Other medicines and Acme Product"/>
              <code>
                <coding>
                  <system value="http://spor.ema.europa.eu/v1/example-sections"/>
                  <code value="9"/>
                  <display value="Other medicines and X"/>
                </coding>
              </code>
              <text>
                <status value="additional"/>
                <div xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1999/xhtml">
                                    <p style="margin-right:-.1pt;line-height:normal;page-break-after:  avoid" class="MsoNormal">
                                        <span lang="EN-GB">Tell your doctor or pharmacist if you are
                                            taking, have recently taken or might take any other
                                            medicines.</span>
                                    </p>
                                    <p style="margin-right:-.1pt;line-height:normal" class="MsoNormal"/>
                                    <p style="margin-right:-.1pt;line-height:normal;page-break-after:  avoid" class="MsoNormal">
                                        <span lang="EN-GB">In particular, tell your doctor if you
                                            are taking the following:</span>
                                    </p>
                                    <p style="margin-right:-.1pt;line-height:normal;page-break-after:  avoid" class="MsoNormal"/>
                                    <p style="margin-left:28.35pt;text-indent:-28.35pt;line-height:  normal;page-break-after:avoid" class="MsoNormal">
                                        <span lang="EN-GB">-</span>
                                        <b>
                                            <span lang="EN-GB">Dimethyl fumarate or other
                                                fumarates.</span>
                                        </b>
                                        <span lang="EN-GB">The active ingredient in Acme Product,
                                            dimethyl fumarate, is also used in other medicines such
                                            as tablets, ointments and baths. You must avoid using
                                            other products that contain fumarates to prevent taking
                                            too much.</span>
                                    </p>
                                    <p style="margin-left:28.35pt;text-indent:-28.35pt;line-height:  normal" class="MsoNormal">
                                        <span lang="EN-GB">-</span>
                                        <b>
                                            <span lang="EN-GB">Other medicines used to treat
                                                psoriasis,</span>
                                        </b>
                                        <span lang="EN-GB">such as methotrexate, retinoids,
                                            psoralens, ciclosporin, or other immunosuppressants or
                                            cytostatics </span>
                                        <span lang="EN-GB">(medicines that affect the immune
                                            system)</span>
                                        <span lang="EN-GB">. Taking these medicines with Acme
                                            Product could increase the risk of side effects on your
                                            immune system.</span>
                                    </p>
                                    <p style="margin-left:28.35pt;text-indent:-28.35pt;line-height:  normal" class="MsoNormal">
                                        <span lang="EN-GB">-</span>
                                        <b>
                                            <span lang="EN-GB">Other medicines that can affect your
                                                kidney function, </span>
                                        </b>
                                        <span lang="EN-GB">such as methotrexate or ciclosporin (used
                                            to treat psoriasis), aminoglycosides (used to treat
                                            infections), diuretics (which increase urine),
                                            nonsteroidal anti‑inflammatory drugs (used to treat
                                            pain) or lithium (used for bipolar disease and
                                            depression). These medicines taken togetherwith Acme
                                            Product could increase the risk of side effects on your
                                            kidneys.</span>
                                    </p>
                                    <p style="line-height:normal" class="MsoNormal"/>
                                    <p style="line-height:normal" class="MsoNormal">
                                        <span lang="EN-GB">If you get severe or prolonged diarrhoea
                                            with Acme Product, other medicines may not work as well
                                            as they should. Talk to your doctor if you have bad
                                            diarrhoea and are concerned that other medicines you are
                                            taking might not work. In particular, if you are taking
                                            a contraceptive medicine (the pill), the effect may be
                                            reduced and you may need to use other barrier methods to
                                            prevent pregnancy.</span>See the instructions in the
                                        patient leaflet of the contraceptive you are taking.
                                    </p>
                                    <p style="line-height:normal" class="MsoNormal"/>
                                    <p style="line-height:normal" class="MsoNormal">
                                        <span lang="EN-GB">If you need a vaccination, talk to your
                                            doctor. Certain types of vaccines (live vaccines) may
                                            cause infection if used during treatment with Acme
                                            Product. Your doctor can advise you what would be
                                            best.</span>
                                    </p>
                                    <p style="line-height:normal" class="MsoNormal"/>
                                </div>
              </text>
            </section>
            <section id="ee8fed00-ef75-4faa-9ce6-796cf7faf49e">
              <title value="Acme Product with alcohol"/>
              <code>
                <coding>
                  <system value="http://spor.ema.europa.eu/v1/example-sections"/>
                  <code value="10"/>
                  <display
                           value="X with &lt;food&gt; &lt;and&gt; &lt;,&gt; &lt;drink&gt; &lt;and&gt; &lt;alcohol&gt;"/>
                </coding>
              </code>
              <text>
                <status value="additional"/>
                <div xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1999/xhtml">
                                    <p style="line-height:normal;page-break-after:avoid" class="MsoNormal">
                                        <span lang="EN-GB">Avoid strong alcoholic drinks (more than
                                            50 ml of spirits containing more than 30% alcohol by
                                            volume) during treatment with Acme Product, as alcohol
                                            can interact with this medicine. This could cause
                                            stomach and intestinal problems.</span>
                                    </p>
                                    <p style="line-height:normal" class="MsoNormal"/>
                                </div>
              </text>
            </section>
            <section id="789f2ac5-8436-4bbf-8384-04daf02273f8">
              <title value="Pregnancy and breast-feeding"/>
              <code>
                <coding>
                  <system value="http://spor.ema.europa.eu/v1/example-sections"/>
                  <code value="11"/>
                  <display
                           value="Pregnancy &lt;and&gt; &lt;,&gt; breast-feeding &lt;and fertility&gt;"/>
                </coding>
              </code>
              <text>
                <status value="additional"/>
                <div xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1999/xhtml">
                                    <p style="line-height:normal;page-break-after:avoid" class="MsoNormal">
                                        <span lang="EN-GB">Do not take Acme Product if you are
                                            pregnant or trying to become pregnant, as Acme Product
                                            may harm your baby. Use effective methods of
                                            contraception to avoid becoming pregnant during
                                            treatment with Acme Product (see also “Other medicines
                                            and Acme Product” above).</span>
                                    </p>
                                    <p style="line-height:normal" class="MsoNormal">
                                        <span lang="EN-GB">Do not breast-feed during treatment with
                                            Acme Product.</span>
                                    </p>
                                    <p style="line-height:normal" class="MsoNormal"/>
                                </div>
              </text>
            </section>
            <section id="98488f54-5cc8-4645-9260-4aba338f55ec">

                                        <span lang="EN-GB">Acme Product </span>
                                        <span lang="EN-GB">may have a minor </span>
                                        <span lang="EN-GB">influence on the ability to drive and use
                                            machines</span>

                                            taking Acme Product. If you are affected, be careful

          <section id="c5b7abf4-708a-44f0-8f25-071b22d3a9e9">
            <title value="3.       How to take Acme Product"/>
            <code>
              <coding>
                <system value="http://spor.ema.europa.eu/v1/example-sections"/>
                <code value="14"/>
                <display value="3. How to &lt;take&gt; &lt;use&gt; X"/>
              </coding>
            </code>
            <text>
              <status value="additional"/>
              <div xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1999/xhtml">
                                <p style="margin-right:-.1pt;line-height:normal;page-break-after:  avoid" class="MsoNormal"/>
                                <p style="margin-right:-.1pt;line-height:normal;page-break-after:  avoid" class="MsoNormal">
                                    <span lang="EN-GB">Always take this medicine exactly as your
                                        doctor or pharmacist has told you. Check with your doctor or
                                        pharmacist if you are not sure.</span>
                                </p>
                                <p style="margin-right:-.1pt;line-height:normal" class="MsoNormal"/>
                                <p style="margin-right:-.1pt;line-height:normal;page-break-after:  avoid" class="MsoNormal">
                                    <b>
                                        <span lang="EN-GB">Dose</span>
                                    </b>
                                </p>
                                <p style="margin-right:-.1pt;line-height:normal;page-break-after:  avoid" class="MsoNormal">
                                    <span lang="EN-GB">Your doctor will start your treatment with a
                                        low dose (using 30 mg Acme Product tablets). This helps to
                                        reduce stomach problems and other side effects. Your dose
                                        will be increased every week as shown in the table below
                                        (switching to 120 mg Acme Product tablets from week 4
                                        onwards).</span>
                                </p>
                                <p style="margin-right:-.1pt;line-height:normal" class="MsoNormal"/>
                                <table border="1" cellpadding="0" cellspacing="0" width="101%" style="border-collapse:collapse;border:none" class="Tablanormal">
                                    <tr style="height:20.8pt">
                                        <td rowspan="2" width="12%" style="width:12.7%;border:solid windowtext 1.0pt;    padding:0in 5.4pt 0in 5.4pt;height:20.8pt">
                                            <p style="text-align:center;line-height:normal" align="center" class="MsoNormal">
                                                <span lang="EN-GB">Treatment week</span>
                                            </p>
                                        </td>
                                        <td rowspan="2" width="13%" style="width:13.42%;border:solid windowtext 1.0pt;    border-left:none;padding:0in 5.4pt 0in 5.4pt;height:20.8pt">
                                            <p style="text-align:center;line-height:normal" align="center" class="MsoNormal">
                                                <span lang="EN-GB">Tablet strength</span>

                                        <td width="15%" style="width:15.72%;border-top:none;border-left:none;    border-bottom:solid windowtext 1.0pt;border-right:solid windowtext 1.0pt;    padding:0in 5.4pt 0in 5.4pt;height:21.15pt">
                                            <p style="text-align:center;line-height:normal" align="center" class="MsoNormal">
                                                <span lang="EN-GB">2</span>
                                            </p>
                                        </td>
                                        <td width="16%" style="width:16.62%;border-top:none;border-left:none;    border-bottom:solid windowtext 1.0pt;border-right:solid windowtext 1.0pt;    padding:0in 5.4pt 0in 5.4pt;height:21.15pt">
                                            <p style="text-align:center;line-height:normal" align="center" class="MsoNormal">
                                                <span lang="EN-GB">5</span>
                                            </p>
                                        </td>
                                        <td width="13%" style="width:13.6%;border-top:none;border-left:none;    border-bottom:solid windowtext 1.0pt;border-right:solid windowtext 1.0pt;    padding:0in 5.4pt 0in 5.4pt;height:21.15pt">
                                            <p style="text-align:center;line-height:normal" align="center" class="MsoNormal">
                                                <span lang="EN-GB">600 mg</span>
                                            </p>
                                        </td>
                                    </tr>
                                    <tr style="height:21.15pt">
                                        <td width="12%" style="width:12.7%;border:solid windowtext 1.0pt;border-top:    none;padding:0in 5.4pt 0in 5.4pt;height:21.15pt">
                                            <p style="text-align:center;line-height:normal" align="center" class="MsoNormal">
                                                <span lang="EN-GB">9+</span>
                                            </p>
                                        </td>
                                        <td width="13%" style="width:13.42%;border-top:none;border-left:none;    border-bottom:solid windowtext 1.0pt;border-right:solid windowtext 1.0pt;    padding:0in 5.4pt 0in 5.4pt;height:21.15pt">
                                            <p style="text-align:center;line-height:normal" align="center" class="MsoNormal">
                                                <span lang="EN-GB">120 mg</span>
                                            </p>
                                        </td>
                                        <td width="14%" style="width:14.7%;border-top:none;border-left:none;    border-bottom:solid windowtext 1.0pt;border-right:solid windowtext 1.0pt;    padding:0in 5.4pt 0in 5.4pt;height:21.15pt">
                                            <p style="text-align:center;line-height:normal" align="center" class="MsoNormal">
                                                <span lang="EN-GB">2</span>
                                            </p>
                                        </td>
                                        <td width="13%" style="width:13.22%;border-top:none;border-left:none;    border-bottom:solid windowtext 1.0pt;border-right:solid windowtext 1.0pt;    padding:0in 5.4pt 0in 5.4pt;height:21.15pt">
                                            <p style="text-align:center;line-height:normal" align="center" class="MsoNormal">
                                                <span lang="EN-GB">2</span>
                                            </p>
                                        </td>
                                        <td width="15%" style="width:15.72%;border-top:none;border-left:none;    border-bottom:solid windowtext 1.0pt;border-right:solid windowtext 1.0pt;    padding:0in 5.4pt 0in 5.4pt;height:21.15pt">
                                            <p style="text-align:center;line-height:normal" align="center" class="MsoNormal">
                                                <span lang="EN-GB">2</span>
                                            </p>
                                        </td>
                                        <td width="16%" style="width:16.62%;border-top:none;border-left:none;    border-bottom:solid windowtext 1.0pt;border-right:solid windowtext 1.0pt;    padding:0in 5.4pt 0in 5.4pt;height:21.15pt">
                                            <p style="text-align:center;line-height:normal" align="center" class="MsoNormal">
                                                <span lang="EN-GB">6</span>
                                            </p>
                                        </td>
                                        <td width="13%" style="width:13.6%;border-top:none;border-left:none;    border-bottom:solid windowtext 1.0pt;border-right:solid windowtext 1.0pt;    padding:0in 5.4pt 0in 5.4pt;height:21.15pt">
                                            <p style="text-align:center;line-height:normal" align="center" class="MsoNormal">
                                                <span lang="EN-GB">720 mg</span>
                                            </p>
                                        </td>
                                    </tr>
                                </table>
                                <p style="text-align:justify;text-justify:inter-ideograph;  line-height:normal" class="MsoNormal"/>
                                <p style="line-height:normal" class="MsoNormal">
                                    <span lang="EN-GB">Your doctor will check how well your
                                        condition is improving after you start taking Acme Product
                                        and will check for side effects. If you have severe side
                                        effects after an increase in dose, your doctor may recommend
                                        that you temporarily go back to the last dose. If the side
                                        effects are not troublesome, your dose will be increased
                                        until your condition is well controlled. You may not need
                                        the maximum dose of 720 mg per day.</span>
                                    <span lang="EN-GB">After your condition has improved
                                        sufficiently, your doctor will consider how to gradually
                                        reduce the daily dose of Acme Product to what you need to
                                        maintain your improvement.</span>
                                </p>
                                <p style="line-height:normal" class="MsoNormal"/>
                                <p style="margin-right:-.1pt;line-height:normal;page-break-after:  avoid" class="MsoNormal">
                                    <b>
                                        <span lang="EN-GB">Method of administration</span>
                                    </b>
                                </p>
                                <p style="line-height:normal;page-break-after:avoid" class="MsoNormal">
                                    <span lang="EN-GB">Swallow Acme Product tablets whole with
                                        liquid. Take your tablets during or immediately after a
                                        meal. Do not crush, break, dissolve or chew your tablets, as
                                        they have a special coating to help prevent irritation of
                                        your stomach.</span>
                                </p>
                                <p style="line-height:normal" class="MsoNormal"/>
                            </div>
            </text>

                                        <span lang="EN-GB">If you think you have taken too many Acme
                                            Product tablets, talk to your doctor or
                                            pharmacist.</span>
                                    </p>
                                    <p style="line-height:normal" class="MsoNormal"/>
                                </div>

            <section id="fb52b9e8-b7d3-4515-bf08-83ffe51f035e">
              <title value="If you forget to take Acme Product"/>
              <code>
                <coding>
                  <system value="http://spor.ema.europa.eu/v1/example-sections"/>
                  <code value="17"/>
                  <display
                           value="If you forget to &lt;take&gt; &lt;use&gt; X&gt;"/>
                </coding>
              </code>
              <text>

                <div xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1999/xhtml">
                                    <p style="margin-right:-.1pt;line-height:normal;page-break-after:  avoid" class="MsoNormal">
                                        <span lang="EN-GB">Do not take a double dose to make up for
                                            a forgotten dose. Take the next dose at the usual time
                                            and continue taking the medicine exactly as described in
                                            this leaflet or exactly as agreed with your doctor.
                                            Please ask your doctor or pharmacist if you are not
                                            sure.</span>
                                    </p>
                                    <p style="margin-right:-1.45pt;line-height:normal" class="MsoNormal"/>
                                    <p style="margin-right:-.1pt;line-height:normal" class="MsoNormal">
                                        <span lang="EN-GB">If you have any further questions on the
                                            use of this medicine, ask your doctor or
                                            pharmacist.</span>
                                    </p>
                                    <p style="margin-right:-.1pt;line-height:normal" class="MsoNormal"/>
                                    <p style="margin-top:0in;margin-right:-.1pt;margin-bottom:0in;  margin-left:28.35pt;margin-bottom:.0001pt;text-indent:-28.35pt;line-height:  normal" class="MsoNormal"/>

          <section id="bbacd6c3-846e-4fa3-bbf5-ed7ed2009837">
            <title value="4.       Possible side effects"/>
            <code>
              <coding>
                <system value="http://spor.ema.europa.eu/v1/example-sections"/>
                <code value="19"/>
                <display value="4. Possible side effects"/>
              </coding>
            </code>
            <text>
              <status value="additional"/>
              <div xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1999/xhtml">
                                <p style="margin-right:-1.45pt;line-height:normal;page-break-after:  avoid" class="MsoNormal"/>
                                <p style="margin-right:-1.45pt;line-height:normal;page-break-after:  avoid" class="MsoNormal">
                                    <span lang="EN-GB">Like all medicines, this medicine can cause
                                        side effects, although not everybody gets them. Some of
                                        these side effects, such as reddening of the face or body
                                        (flushing), diarrhoea, stomach problems and nausea usually
                                        improve as you continue treatment.</span>
                                </p>
                                <p style="margin-right:-1.45pt;line-height:normal" class="MsoNormal"/>
                                <p style="margin-right:-1.45pt;line-height:normal" class="MsoNormal">
                                    <span lang="EN-GB">The </span>
                                    <span lang="EN-GB">most serious side effects that may</span>
                                    <span lang="EN-GB">occur with Acme Product are allergic or
                                        hypersensitivity reactions; kidney failure or a kidney
                                        disease called Fanconi syndrome; or a severe brain infection
                                        called progressive multifocal leukoencephalopathy (PML). It
                                        is not known how commonly they occur. For symptoms see
                                        below.</span>
                                </p>
                                <p style="margin-right:-1.45pt;line-height:normal" class="MsoNormal"/>
                                <p style="margin-right:-1.45pt;line-height:normal;page-break-after:  avoid" class="MsoNormal">
                                    <u>
                                        <span lang="EN-GB">Allergic or hypersensitivity
                                            reactions</span>
                                    </u>
                                </p>
                                <p style="margin-right:-1.4pt;line-height:normal;page-break-after:  avoid" class="MsoNormal">
                                    <span lang="EN-GB">Allergic or hypersensitivity reactions are
                                        rare but may be very serious. Reddening of the face or body
                                        (flushing) is a very common side effect </span>
                                    <span lang="EN-GB">which </span>
                                    <span lang="EN-GB">may affect more than 1 in 10 people</span>
                                    <span lang="EN-GB">.</span>
                                    <span lang="EN-GB">However, if you become flushed and get any of
                                        the following signs: </span>
                                </p>
                                <p style="margin-top:0in;margin-right:-1.4pt;  margin-bottom:0in;margin-left:.25in;text-indent:-.25in" class="PrrafodelistaCxSpFirst">
                                    <span style="font-size:11.0pt" lang="EN-GB">-</span>
                                    <span style="font-size:11.0pt" lang="EN-GB">wheezing, difficulty
                                        breathing or shortness of breath,</span>
                                </p>
                                <p style="margin-top:0in;margin-right:-1.4pt;  margin-bottom:0in;margin-left:.25in;text-indent:-.25in" class="PrrafodelistaCxSpLast">
                                    <span style="font-size:11.0pt" lang="EN-GB">-</span>
                                    <span style="font-size:11.0pt" lang="EN-GB">swelling of the
                                        face, lips, mouth or tongue </span>
                                </p>
                                <p style="margin-right:-1.4pt;line-height:normal" class="MsoNormal">
                                    <span lang="EN-GB">stop taking Acme Product and call a doctor
                                        straight away.</span>
                                </p>
                                <p style="margin-right:-1.45pt;line-height:normal" class="MsoNormal"/>
                                <p style="margin-right:-.1pt;line-height:normal;page-break-after:  avoid" class="MsoNormal">
                                    <u>
                                        <span lang="EN-GB">Brain infection called PML</span>
                                    </u>
                                </p>
                                <p style="line-height:normal;page-break-after:avoid" class="MsoNormal">
                                    <span lang="EN-GB">Progressive multifocal leukoencephalopathy
                                        (PML) is a rare but serious brain infection that can lead to
                                        severe disability or death. If you notice new or worsening
                                        weakness on one side of the body; clumsiness; changes in
                                        vision, thinking or memory; confusion; or personality
                                        changes lasting several days, stop taking Acme Product and
                                        talk to your doctor straight away.</span>
                                </p>
                                <p style="line-height:normal;text-autospace:none" class="MsoNormal"/>
                                <p style="margin-right:-.1pt;line-height:normal;page-break-after:  avoid" class="MsoNormal">
                                    <u>
                                        <span lang="EN-GB">Fanconi syndrome</span>
                                    </u>
                                </p>
                                <p style="margin-right:-.1pt;line-height:normal;page-break-after:  avoid" class="MsoNormal">
                                    <span lang="EN-GB">Fanconi syndrome is a rare but serious kidney
                                        disorder which may occur with Acme Product. If you notice
                                        you are passing more urine, are more thirsty and drinking
                                        more than normal, your muscles seem weaker, you break a
                                        bone, or just have aches and pains, talk to your doctor as
                                        soon as possible so that this can be investigated
                                        further.</span>
                                </p>
                                <p style="margin-right:-1.45pt;line-height:normal" class="MsoNormal"/>
                                <p style="margin-right:-1.45pt;line-height:normal" class="MsoNormal">
                                    <span lang="EN-GB">Talk to your doctor if you get any of the
                                        following side effects.</span>
                                </p>
                                <p style="margin-right:-1.45pt;line-height:normal" class="MsoNormal"/>
                                <p style="margin-right:-.1pt;line-height:normal;page-break-after:  avoid" class="MsoNormal">
                                    <span lang="EN-GB">Very common side effects (may affect more
                                        than 1 in 10 people):</span>
                                </p>
                                <p style="margin-left:28.35pt;text-indent:-28.35pt;line-height:  normal;page-break-after:avoid" class="MsoNormal">
                                    <span lang="EN-GB">-</span>
                                    <span lang="EN-GB">decrease in white blood cells called
                                        lymphocytes (lymphopenia)</span>
                                </p>
                                <p style="margin-left:28.35pt;text-indent:-28.35pt;line-height:  normal" class="MsoNormal">
                                    <span lang="EN-GB">-</span>
                                    <span lang="EN-GB">decrease in all white blood cells
                                        (leukopenia)</span>
                                </p>
                                <p style="margin-left:28.35pt;text-indent:-28.35pt;line-height:  normal" class="MsoNormal">
                                    <span lang="EN-GB">-</span>
                                    <span lang="EN-GB">reddening of the face or body
                                        (flushing)</span>
                                </p>
                                <p style="margin-left:28.35pt;text-indent:-28.35pt;line-height:  normal" class="MsoNormal">
                                    <span lang="EN-GB">-</span>
                                    <span lang="EN-GB">diarrhoea</span>
                                </p>
                                <p style="margin-left:28.35pt;text-indent:-28.35pt;line-height:  normal" class="MsoNormal">
                                    <span lang="EN-GB">-</span>
                                    <span lang="EN-GB">bloating, stomach pain or stomach
                                        cramps</span>
                                </p>
                                <p style="margin-left:28.35pt;text-indent:-28.35pt;line-height:  normal" class="MsoNormal">
                                    <span lang="EN-GB">-</span>
                                    <span lang="EN-GB">feeling sick (nausea)</span>
                                </p>
                                <p style="margin-right:-.1pt;line-height:normal" class="MsoNormal"/>
                                <p style="margin-right:-.1pt;line-height:normal;page-break-after:  avoid" class="MsoNormal">
                                    <span lang="EN-GB">Common side effects (may affect up to 1 in 10
                                        people):</span>
                                </p>
                                <p style="margin-left:28.35pt;text-indent:-28.35pt;line-height:  normal;page-break-after:avoid" class="MsoNormal">
                                    <span lang="EN-GB">-</span>
                                    <span lang="EN-GB">increase in all white blood cells
                                        (leukocytosis)</span>
                                </p>
                                <p style="margin-left:28.35pt;text-indent:-28.35pt;line-height:  normal" class="MsoNormal">
                                    <span lang="EN-GB">-</span>
                                    <span lang="EN-GB">increase in specific white blood cells called
                                        eosinophils</span>
                                </p>
                                <p style="margin-left:28.35pt;text-indent:-28.35pt;line-height:  normal" class="MsoNormal">
                                    <span lang="EN-GB">-</span>
                                    <span lang="EN-GB">increase in certain enzymes in the blood
                                        (used for checking the health of your liver)</span>
                                </p>
                                <p style="margin-left:28.35pt;text-indent:-28.35pt;line-height:  normal" class="MsoNormal">
                                    <span lang="EN-GB">-</span>
                                    <span lang="EN-GB">being sick </span>
                                </p>
                                <p style="margin-left:28.35pt;text-indent:-28.35pt;line-height:  normal" class="MsoNormal">
                                    <span lang="EN-GB">-</span>
                                    <span lang="EN-GB">constipation</span>
                                </p>
                                <p style="margin-left:28.35pt;text-indent:-28.35pt;line-height:  normal" class="MsoNormal">
                                    <span lang="EN-GB">-</span>
                                    <span lang="EN-GB">gas (flatulence), stomach discomfort,
                                        indigestion</span>
                                </p>
                                <p style="margin-left:28.35pt;text-indent:-28.35pt;line-height:  normal" class="MsoNormal">
                                    <span lang="EN-GB">-</span>
                                    <span lang="EN-GB">decreased appetite</span>
                                </p>
                                <p style="margin-left:28.35pt;text-indent:-28.35pt;line-height:  normal" class="MsoNormal">
                                    <span lang="EN-GB">-</span>
                                    <span lang="EN-GB">headache</span>
                                </p>
                                <p style="margin-left:28.35pt;text-indent:-28.35pt;line-height:  normal" class="MsoNormal">
                                    <span lang="EN-GB">-</span>
                                    <span lang="EN-GB">feeling tired</span>
                                </p>
                                <p style="margin-left:28.35pt;text-indent:-28.35pt;line-height:  normal" class="MsoNormal">
                                    <span lang="EN-GB">-</span>
                                    <span lang="EN-GB">weakness</span>
                                </p>
                                <p style="margin-left:28.35pt;text-indent:-28.35pt;line-height:  normal" class="MsoNormal">
                                    <span lang="EN-GB">-</span>
                                    <span lang="EN-GB">feeling hot</span>
                                </p>
                                <p style="margin-left:28.35pt;text-indent:-28.35pt;line-height:  normal" class="MsoNormal">
                                    <span lang="EN-GB">-</span>
                                    <span lang="EN-GB">abnormal sensations of the skin, such as
                                        itching, burning, stinging, tickling or tingling</span>
                                </p>
                                <p style="margin-left:28.35pt;text-indent:-28.35pt;line-height:  normal" class="MsoNormal">
                                    <span lang="EN-GB">-</span>
                                    <span lang="EN-GB">pink or red blotches on the skin
                                        (erythema)</span>
                                </p>
                                <p style="margin-right:-1.45pt;line-height:normal" class="MsoNormal"/>
                                <p style="margin-right:-1.45pt;line-height:normal;page-break-after:  avoid" class="MsoNormal">
                                    <span lang="EN-GB">Uncommon side effects (may affect up to 1 in
                                        100 people):</span>
                                </p>
                                <p style="margin-left:28.35pt;text-indent:-28.35pt;line-height:  normal;page-break-after:avoid" class="MsoNormal">
                                    <span lang="EN-GB">-</span>
                                    <span lang="EN-GB">dizziness</span>
                                </p>
                                <p style="margin-left:28.35pt;text-indent:-28.35pt;line-height:  normal" class="MsoNormal">
                                    <span lang="EN-GB">-</span>
                                    <span lang="EN-GB">excess protein in the urine
                                        (proteinuria)</span>
                                </p>
                                <p style="margin-left:28.35pt;text-indent:-28.35pt;line-height:  normal" class="MsoNormal">
                                    <span lang="EN-GB">-</span>
                                    <span lang="EN-GB">increase in serum creatinine (a substance in
                                        the blood used for measuring how well your kidneys are
                                        working)</span>
                                </p>
                                <p style="line-height:normal" class="MsoNormal"/>
                                <p style="line-height:normal;page-break-after:avoid" class="MsoNormal">
                                    <span lang="EN-GB">Rare side effects (may affect up to 1 in
                                        1,000 people):</span>
                                </p>
                                <p style="line-height:normal;page-break-after:avoid" class="MsoNormal">
                                    <span lang="EN-GB">- allergic skin reaction</span>
                                </p>
                                <p style="line-height:normal" class="MsoNormal"/>
                                <p style="line-height:normal;page-break-after:avoid" class="MsoNormal">
                                    <span lang="EN-GB">Very rare side effects (may affect up to 1 in
                                        10,000 people):</span>
                                </p>
                                <p style="line-height:normal;page-break-after:avoid" class="MsoNormal">
                                    <span lang="EN-GB">- acute lymphatic leukaemia (a type of blood
                                        cancer)</span>
                                </p>
                                <p style="line-height:normal" class="MsoNormal">
                                    <span lang="EN-GB">- decrease in all types of blood cells
                                        (pancytopenia)</span>
                                </p>
                                <p style="line-height:normal" class="MsoNormal"/>
                                <p style="line-height:normal" class="MsoNormal">
                                    <span style="color:black">Frequency not known (frequency cannot
                                        be estimated from the available data):</span>
                                </p>
                                <p style="line-height:normal" class="MsoNormal">
                                    <span lang="EN-GB">- shingles</span>
                                </p>
                                <p style="line-height:normal" class="MsoNormal"/>
                            </div>
            </text>
            <section id="54ec3d9e-f6f1-40ae-a049-61f8d2462b1b">
              <title value="Reporting of side effects"/>
              <code>
                <coding>
                  <system value="http://spor.ema.europa.eu/v1/example-sections"/>
                  <code value="21"/>
                  <display value="Reporting of side effects"/>
                </coding>
              </code>
              <text>
                <status value="additional"/>
                <div xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1999/xhtml">
                                    <p style="margin-bottom:0in;line-height:normal;page-break-after:  avoid" class="BodytextAgency">
                                        <span style="font-size:11.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;,serif" lang="EN-GB">If you get any side effects, talk to your
                                            doctor or pharmacist.This includes any possible side
                                            effects not listed in this leaflet. You can also report
                                            side effects directly via
                                            <span style="background:lightgrey">the national reporting
                                                system listed in </span>
                                        </span>
                                        <span lang="EN-GB">
                                            <a href="http://www.ema.europa.eu/docs/en_GB/document_library/Template_or_form/2013/03/WC500139752.doc">
                                                <span style="font-size:11.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;,serif;color:blue;  background:lightgrey">Appendix V</span>
                                            </a>
                                        </span>
                                        <span style="font-size:11.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;,serif" lang="EN-GB">. By reporting side effects you can help
                                            provide more information on the safety of this
                                            medicine.</span>
                                    </p>
                                    <p style="margin-top:0in;margin-right:-.1pt;margin-bottom:0in;  margin-left:28.35pt;margin-bottom:.0001pt;text-indent:-28.35pt;line-height:  normal" class="MsoNormal"/>
                                    <p style="margin-top:0in;margin-right:-.1pt;margin-bottom:0in;  margin-left:28.35pt;margin-bottom:.0001pt;text-indent:-28.35pt;line-height:  normal" class="MsoNormal"/>
                                </div>
              </text>

          <section id="b9d4e42c-a17e-49f4-a1de-435554eb697b">
            <title value="5.       How to store Acme Product"/>
            <code>
              <coding>
                <system value="http://spor.ema.europa.eu/v1/example-sections"/>
                <code value="22"/>
                <display value="5. How to store X"/>
              </coding>
            </code>
            <text>
              <status value="additional"/>
              <div xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1999/xhtml">
                                <p style="margin-right:-.1pt;line-height:normal;page-break-after:  avoid" class="MsoNormal"/>
                                <p style="margin-right:-.1pt;line-height:normal;page-break-after:  avoid" class="MsoNormal">
                                    <span lang="EN-GB">Keep this medicine out of the sight and reach
                                        of children.</span>
                                </p>
                                <p style="margin-right:-.1pt;line-height:normal" class="MsoNormal"/>
                                <p style="margin-right:-.1pt;line-height:normal" class="MsoNormal">
                                    <span lang="EN-GB">Do not use this medicine after the expiry
                                        date which is stated on the carton </span>
                                    <span lang="EN-GB">and the blister after “EXP”. The expiry date
                                        refers to the last day of that month.</span>
                                </p>
                                <p style="margin-right:-.1pt;line-height:normal" class="MsoNormal"/>
                                <p style="margin-left:28.35pt;text-indent:-28.35pt;line-height:  normal" class="MsoNormal">
                                    <span lang="EN-GB">This medicine does not require any special
                                        storage conditions.</span>
                                </p>
                                <p style="margin-left:28.35pt;text-indent:-28.35pt;line-height:  normal" class="MsoNormal"/>
                                <p style="margin-right:-.1pt;line-height:normal" class="MsoNormal">
                                    <span lang="EN-GB">Do not throw away any medicines via
                                        wastewater or household waste. Ask your pharmacist how to
                                        throw away medicines you no longer use. These measures will
                                        help protect the environment.</span>
                                </p>
                                <p style="margin-right:-.1pt;line-height:normal" class="MsoNormal"/>
                                <p style="margin-right:-.1pt;line-height:normal" class="MsoNormal"/>
                            </div>
            </text>
          </section>
          <section id="4e7d99cb-9110-4e03-b4c7-2a23ba816efb">
            <title value="6.       Contents of the pack and other information"/>
            <code>
              <coding>
                <system value="http://spor.ema.europa.eu/v1/example-sections"/>
                <code value="23"/>
                <display value="6. Contents of the pack and other information"/>
              </coding>
            </code>
            <text>
              <status value="additional"/>
              <div xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1999/xhtml">
                                <p style="margin-right:-.1pt;line-height:normal" class="MsoNormal"/>
                                <p style="margin-right:-.1pt;line-height:normal" class="MsoNormal">
                                    <b>
                                        <span lang="EN-GB">What Acme Product 30 mg contains</span>
                                    </b>
                                </p>
                                <p style="margin-left:28.35pt;text-indent:-28.35pt;line-height:  normal" class="MsoNormal">
                                    <span lang="EN-GB">-</span>
                                    <span lang="EN-GB">the active substance is dimethyl fumarate.
                                        One tablet contains 30 mg dimethyl fumarate.</span>
                                </p>
                                <p style="margin-left:28.35pt;text-indent:-28.35pt;line-height:  normal" class="MsoNormal">
                                    <span lang="EN-GB">-</span>
                                    <span lang="EN-GB">the other ingredients are: lactose
                                        monohydrate, cellulose microcrystalline, croscarmellose
                                        sodium, colloidal anhydrous silica, magnesium stearate,
                                        methacrylic acid‑ethyl acrylate copolymer (1:1), talc,
                                        triethyl citrate, titanium dioxide (E171) and
                                        simethicone.</span>
                                </p>
                                <p style="margin-right:-.1pt;line-height:normal" class="MsoNormal"/>
                                <p style="margin-right:-.1pt;line-height:normal;page-break-after:  avoid" class="MsoNormal">
                                    <b>
                                        <span lang="EN-GB">What Acme Product 30 mg looks like and
                                            contents of the pack</span>
                                    </b>
                                </p>
                                <p style="margin-right:-.1pt;line-height:normal;page-break-after:  avoid" class="MsoNormal">
                                    <span lang="EN-GB">Acme Product 30 mg is a </span>
                                    <span lang="EN-GB">white, round </span>
                                    <span lang="EN-GB">tablet</span>
                                    <span lang="EN-GB">with a diameter of approximately 6.8
                                        mm.</span>
                                </p>
                                <p style="margin-right:-.1pt;line-height:normal" class="MsoNormal">
                                    <a name="_Hlk9583735">
                                        <span lang="EN-GB">Acme Product 30 mg is available in packs
                                            containing 42, 70 and 210 gastro‑resistant tablets. Not
                                            all pack sizes may be marketed. The tablets are packed
                                            in PVC/PVDC‑aluminium blisters.</span>
                                    </a>
                                </p>
                                <p style="line-height:normal" class="MsoNormal"/>
                            </div>
            </text>

          <section id="a3ddd703-ef3a-49ea-b7a4-a66e1d97b9c3">
            <title value="1.       What Acme Product is and what it is used for"/>
            <code>
              <coding>
                <system value="http://spor.ema.europa.eu/v1/example-sections"/>
                <code value="4"/>
                <display value="1. What X is and what it is used for"/>
              </coding>
            </code>
            <text>
              <status value="additional"/>
              <div xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1999/xhtml">
                                <p style="margin-right:-.1pt;line-height:normal;page-break-after:  avoid" class="MsoNormal"/>
                                <p style="margin-right:-.1pt;line-height:normal;page-break-after:  avoid" class="MsoNormal">
                                    <b>
                                        <span lang="EN-GB">What Acme Product is</span>
                                    </b>
                                </p>
                                <p style="margin-right:-.1pt;line-height:normal;page-break-after:  avoid" class="MsoNormal">
                                    <span lang="EN-GB">Acme Product is a medicine that contains the
                                        active substance dimethyl fumarate. Dimethyl fumarate works
                                        on cells of the immune system (the body's natural defences).
                                        It changes the activity of the immune system and reduces the
                                        production of substances involved in causing
                                        psoriasis.</span>
                                </p>
                                <p style="margin-right:-.1pt;line-height:normal" class="MsoNormal"/>
                                <p style="margin-right:-.1pt;line-height:normal;page-break-after:  avoid" class="MsoNormal">
                                    <b>
                                        <span lang="EN-GB">What Acme Product is used for</span>
                                    </b>
                                </p>
                                <p style="line-height:normal;page-break-after:avoid" class="MsoNormal">
                                    <span lang="EN-GB">Acme Product tablets are used to treat
                                        moderate to severe plaque psoriasis in adults. Psoriasis is
                                        a disease causing thickened, inflamed, red areas on the
                                        skin, often covered by silvery scales.</span>
                                </p>
                                <p style="margin-right:-.1pt;line-height:normal" class="MsoNormal"/>
                                <p style="line-height:normal" class="MsoNormal">
                                    <span lang="EN-GB">Response to Acme Product can be generally
                                        seen as early as week 3 and improves over time. Experience
                                        with related products containing dimethyl fumarate shows
                                        treatment benefit for at least up to 24 months.</span>
                                </p>
                                <p style="margin-right:-.1pt;line-height:normal" class="MsoNormal"/>
                                <p style="margin-right:-.1pt;line-height:normal" class="MsoNormal"/>
                            </div>
            </text>
          </section>
          <section id="f4a9170c-9fa4-4a40-b259-e2c8761939ea">

            <text>
